text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRDCRi92DWI/AAAAAAAACM0/_BJL1h6liSY/s1600/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRDCRi92DWI/AAAAAAAACM0/_BJL1h6liSY/s400/images+%252817%2529.jpg\" width=\"292\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uQBLHR6DdTQ/WuvmavBNAKI/AAAAAAABbDs/NvOj9pXW3RA0nO0OaqoJPEiNtmpy_ftYACLcBGAs/s1600/BrMuQWs_Amravati.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"263\" data-original-width=\"350\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-uQBLHR6DdTQ/WuvmavBNAKI/AAAAAAABbDs/NvOj9pXW3RA0nO0OaqoJPEiNtmpy_ftYACLcBGAs/s640/BrMuQWs_Amravati.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRDCVP1rEVI/AAAAAAAACM4/UayxBDAYEH8/s1600/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"278\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRDCVP1rEVI/AAAAAAAACM4/UayxBDAYEH8/s400/images+%252816%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">I stayed in London for 2 weeks for briefing , prior joining a British flagged ship. (By the way this Stainless steel Chemical tanker , St James Park was with the Somalian pirates for several months.)</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Every day I used to walk down from my hotel at Tavishtock square , to the British Museum-- just a few minutes walk.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Every year 7 million people visit this greatest universal museum of the world which was established in 1753 , and now contain more than 13 million objects.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Every single day , as soon as I entered the building some sort of feeling would possess me. I had the same feeling on all the days. It was a mixture of nostalgia, rage , shame . Hacked off and broken statue faces, limbs, noses lay every where .</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">It was the equivalent of you , coming across a beautiful woman with long hair. And soon enough her chopped off nose, long hair and breasts lands up for display in a glass cage, leaving her faceless, bald , breast less and dead. The rationale being --\" See her hair and breasts were NOT safe on her own body!, We saved it \"</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;\">And now-- wonder of wonders-- using this chopped off hair and tit-- Rothschild and Vatican has been rewriting th history of the planet. \" See when we look at the tit objectively, from this angle, we can deduce that&nbsp;this woman had two childern BLAH BLAH\" &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FlzweE4ORBY/TkTeL0thd_I/AAAAAAAAFSM/OfG5Gn3TSAg/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-FlzweE4ORBY/TkTeL0thd_I/AAAAAAAAFSM/OfG5Gn3TSAg/s1600/untitled.png\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">95% of the artifacts in the British Museum are stolen and vandalized objects , and not as the greedy British historians would like us to believe that they were gifts or given for safe keeping.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">I remember feeling physically overwhelmed by the sheer scale and variety of the artifacts, art and ideas on display:</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;5000 year old Mesopotamian relics, &nbsp;Roman statuary, &nbsp;Pharaonic carvings, &nbsp;Viking burial objects , &nbsp;Indian Buddhist treasures, &nbsp; Babylonian Antiques, The Greek Apollo temple frieze, &nbsp;the Turkish Halicarnassus sculptures, &nbsp;Chinese ceramics , Ur Mesopotamian goldenware---</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">They hardly gave importance to the vedic idols. <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">The vedic civilisation is the worlds first civilisation. &nbsp;It flourished on the banks of the river Saraswati from 9000 BC to 4000 BC</span>, till the river dried up due to tectonic shifts blocking the Himalayan glacial mouth.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">-- I wandered, blinking, from room to room.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The priceless Egyptian Rosetta stone, &nbsp;vandalized Parthenon marbles, &nbsp;Benin Bronzes, Ethopian tabots and royal crown , Tajikistan treasures, &nbsp;broken busts of Ramses II, &nbsp;Amenhotep III , the 8 foot tall bronze Buddha sakyamuni ( ridiculously renamed as Birmingham Buddha ), &nbsp;the &nbsp;Amaravati stupa railings , &nbsp;the Assyrian black obelisk, &nbsp;the Portland vase &nbsp;etc etc.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The museum was not trying to tell me something; it seemed to be offering to tell me everything.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">At the entrance the golden roll of honour of Patrons of the British Museum was displayed . Now who are these so called Lord Elgins in reality ? \u2013 just evil smugglers, looters and vandalisers.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Elgin kept all his stolen greek marble goodies with himself , and sold it to the British museum for 35000 pounds only when his ass was on fire.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">I asked one of the English Captains about the mindless vandalism and brazen display of stolen treasures. I said \u201c If you visit an Indian Museum you will never find stolen treasures and vandalized objects\". He replied \u201c We British have a lot , we are not proud about. We are indeed guilty of stealing culture \u201d .</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">True-- If one has at least some vestige of self-respect one would not seek the possession of anything which belongs to another by right\u201d .</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\"><i>Will the British allow Stonehenge to be vandalized, broken into little pieces and then shipped to the museum of some other country? \u2013 talk about double standards.</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;\"><i>The same British government has made a huge fuss about returning art and treasures stolen by the Nazis during the second world war. &nbsp;But they will not practice what they preach.</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Don't the English have artifacts of their own culture and own history that they can show in museums? Britain can no longer claim a monopoly of civilization and culture. Booty from an occupied land may have been often taken in history, but it's not legal and definitely immoral to hold on to it, when the rightful owners want if back in the 21st century.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">East India Company, who came to India in the year 1612 as traders and soon turned their attention to collecting some of the finest artifacts which they took back as personal possessions. Then they cultivated Opium in Bengal , India and smuggled more than 3000 tons to China , to barter with silver/ tea and to make addicts out of 20 million Chinese -- incl the emperor.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">History repeats itself.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The widespread looting in Baghdad, Basra, Mosul, Kirkuk and other Iraqi cities, following the collapse of the Ba'athist regime of President Saddam Hussein, was not merely an incidental byproduct of the US military conquest of Iraq. It was deliberately encouraged and fostered. Thousands took part in the looting in Baghdad which began , the day the Hussein government ceased to function in the capital city .</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Perhaps the most devastating loss for the Iraqi people is the ransacking of the National Museum, the greatest trove of archaeological and historical artifacts in the Middle East. The 28 galleries of the huge museum were picked clean by looters who made off with more than 171,000 irreplaceable artifacts, relics of past civilizations dating back 8,000 years\n.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">\n</span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: left;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">These included the Sacred\nVase of Warka [ 3200 B.C.], the Mask of Warka [ 3100 B.C.], the Golden Harp of\nUr [ 2500 B.C.], the Bassetki Statue [2250 B.C.], <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>the twin copper Ninhursag Bulls [ca. 2475\nB.C.]. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Also stolen was a spectacular\ncollection of more than 1,000 pieces of gold jewelry and precious stones from\nthe eighth and ninth centuries B.C. that had been discovered between 1988 and\n1990 by Iraqi archaeologist Muzahim Hussein Mahmud during his excavation of\nfour royal tombs, and is considered by many to be one of the greatest\narchaeological finds .</span></span></span></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\">\n</span>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; text-align: left;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The museum's entire card catalog was destroyed, making it impossible even to identify what has been lost . The military stood by toothless.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\"><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The Mesopotamian civilisation along with the Vedic Indian civilisation is the oldest in the world-- what was stolen , were all priceless-- you cant put a US dollar tag on it.</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Donald Rumsfeld famously said . \"All freedom's untidy. Free people are free to make mistakes and commit crimes\u201d .</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;\">Today Rothschild would like you and me to believe , that they only contributed honourable stuff like zoological specimens -- like turtle shells --</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;\">How sweet! </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;\">Sniff!</span></div>\n<div style=\"margin: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "12", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/247388304096041082/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "2068016183039486859", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-12-21T13:17:00+05:30", "updated": "2013-02-18T17:44:41+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzYxMTg5NjgxMDY0Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/12/pumping-systems-on-chemical-tankers.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/2068016183039486859", "title": "PUMPING SYSTEMS ON CHEMICAL TANKERS -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBVJQtjDGI/AAAAAAAACJo/RESVnNcxLYY/s1600/chm.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBVJQtjDGI/AAAAAAAACJo/RESVnNcxLYY/s1600/chm.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">A pump is used to move liquids from lower pressure to higher pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">CENTRIFUGAL </span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">&nbsp;pump</span> is basically a kinetic pump which increases the flow when through the pump\u2014it centrifuges the liquid into the discharge line. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWDjRY7rI/AAAAAAAACJs/vrZDY72j5tY/s1600/CP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWDjRY7rI/AAAAAAAACJs/vrZDY72j5tY/s1600/CP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">If the flow into the pump suction is less than the delivery the pump will cavitate causing gassing and loss of suction. They are resistable to solids in cargo. The big disadvantage is its inability to evacuate air/ gas from its casing. The pump casing must be filled with liquid before starting\u2014the pump must be stopped to do this. When the impeller starts to turn the liquid is driven to the periphery of the housing by centrifugal forces. This results in a positive pressure on the outside of the impeller and a negative pressure in the centre.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/wMyty9y-pHQ/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/wMyty9y-pHQ&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/wMyty9y-pHQ&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWOgzaQRI/AAAAAAAACJ4/mv3rRYKTF_0/s1600/CP2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWOgzaQRI/AAAAAAAACJ4/mv3rRYKTF_0/s1600/CP2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Centrifugal pumps can be operated with dischg valve closed as long as the pump does not grow too hot. The last part of dischg is more effective with pump running at low RPM and against a throttled delivery valve. For hot liquids and those which flash into vapour at pressures below atmospheric pressure, the liquid must flow into the pump suction under positive pressure. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/B8MV09HF-nY/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/B8MV09HF-nY&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/B8MV09HF-nY&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Never run a centrifugal pump dry. The pump bearing temp must not exceed 90C. No liquid will be delivered if the pump rpm is too less when the dischg head is too high or suction lift is too high . The viscosity of liquid cannot be too high. There cannot be any leaks on the suction side pipelines or air leak in the shaft seal or vaporisation in the suction line. Never try to reduce pump capacity by throttling the valve on the suction side. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/Vq3hEe5jzSM/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/Vq3hEe5jzSM&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/Vq3hEe5jzSM&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 279.0pt 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The casings of centrifugal pumps <b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\">without a self priming system</b> should be vented of air or gas and primed full of liquid before starting the pump.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The pump suction valve should be full OPEN and a flow of liquid should be available to the pump suction when the pump is started.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Variable speed pumps should be started with the pump discharge valve closed and as the pump speed is increased the discharge valve should be progressively opened to maintain an appropriate discharge head.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Constant speed pumps should be started with the discharge valve only slightly opened and the discharge valve further adjusted to maintain an appropriate discharge head once the pump has been started.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Control of the capacity of a centrifugal pump can be obtained either by throttling the pump discharge valve (and artificially increasing the total head) or, if possible, by restricting the pump's speed or by a combination of both of these methods.&nbsp; In general for bulk cargo operations it is preferable to throttle the discharge valve only and so maintain the full power of the pump to overcome the head resistance of the terminal piping system. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">This is most important where the pumps are being run at different speeds as the pumps running at the low speeds may have their pumping rates severely restricted by the system discharge head. Certain times it may not discharge at all and are called sleeping pumps.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The pump suction valve must always be full OPEN when the pump is running and this valve must not be throttled to control capacity during operation.&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWKkjVufI/AAAAAAAACJ0/aeGgWbDDAiQ/s1600/CP3.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWKkjVufI/AAAAAAAACJ0/aeGgWbDDAiQ/s1600/CP3.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">In general, the suctions of several centrifugal pumps should not be cross\u2011connected and each pump should take suction individually from its own main suction line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWHy0GyEI/AAAAAAAACJw/Nxdfipi4JUE/s1600/CP4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWHy0GyEI/AAAAAAAACJw/Nxdfipi4JUE/s1600/CP4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">When the liquid level in a tank being pumped out reaches a low level the pump suction condition should be maintained at an adequate value by either cracking open a tank with a higher liquid level or reducing the pump speed.&nbsp; Inadequate suction conditions (high vacuum) will cause cavitation of the pump and possible gassing up and loss of pump suction.&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">DEEPWELL</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"> pumps</span>\u2014are centrifugal pumps. They are self priming as long as the suction well is full. 85% if centrifugal pump pumping problems occur on the suction side. This has been eliminated on deep well pumps which do NOT have a suction pipe. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWluFTCbI/AAAAAAAACJ8/lBLpmTn2KQM/s1600/DW2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWluFTCbI/AAAAAAAACJ8/lBLpmTn2KQM/s1600/DW2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">They are variable speed pumps as their rpm can be manually adjusted from zero to maximum designed speed using the pump\u2019s control lever. The pumps\u2019 hydraulic system (which incorporates a STC ) is so designed that the maximum design speed of the pump cannot be exceeded regardless of the pump suction and discharge conditions. They are thus different from the conventional variable speed centrifugal pumps and over speed trips are neither required nor fitted .<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XZZzNe54baY/USIXwXdxGEI/AAAAAAAAfVQ/U5sbqU8smss/s1600/fgt43w.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-XZZzNe54baY/USIXwXdxGEI/AAAAAAAAfVQ/U5sbqU8smss/s400/fgt43w.jpg\" width=\"237\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">When your run a Framo pump at full speed in a tank of low SG cargo the hyd pressure will be less than a high SG cargo. For the same speed any variation of the pump\u2019s suction and discharge heads will also alter the hydraulic driving pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Increasing the speed control lever setting will increase the driving pressure and reduction will reduce the driving pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">When operating several pumps in parallel , the driving pressure of each pump should be about the same value, lest there is an overflow. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: -1.0in 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Framo pumps are self priming pumps , hence it is not necessary to vent the pump before starting.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: -1.0in 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Since there are no suction lines for deep well pumps, there is no need to consider flow velocities in suction piping .Only the velocities in cargo discharge piping system need be considered when operating at high throughput.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWqAfT8WI/AAAAAAAACKA/QjT1EdSWQyw/s1600/DW.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBWqAfT8WI/AAAAAAAACKA/QjT1EdSWQyw/s1600/DW.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: -1.0in 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The Framo deep well pump may be started with the discharge valve open. However, if other pumps are discharging to the same line, or if there is a standing head of cargo, assuming there are no non-return valves like on Japanese deep well pumps , the opening of this pump\u2019s discharge valve will permit liquid in the piping system to pass into this tank unless the pump is running and discharging. The standard procedure shall therefore be to start the pump with the discharge valve CLOSED.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">RECIPROCATING</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"> pumps </span>can apply unlimited delivery pressure \u2013the limit being set by the size and solidness of the pump. It does not have to be filled with liquid prior pumping starts. Air/ gas is evacuated from the suction side of the pump. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBXfhz9mRI/AAAAAAAACKE/vslg-g2gMMk/s1600/RP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBXfhz9mRI/AAAAAAAACKE/vslg-g2gMMk/s1600/RP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The pump delivers pulsating flow \u2013double acting pumps are less pulsating . In order to smooth en the flow and to make the flow constant , air vessels are uses on the suction/ delivery side \u2013they act as accumulator dampers as long as they have air inside them for the air cushion. The acceleration is now restricted to the space between the air vessels. If the acceleration and deceleration inside the suction pipes are too much, the result is cavitation and vibrations. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/ZezYPfJUpIg/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/ZezYPfJUpIg&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/ZezYPfJUpIg&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">They are sensitive to solids in cargo. Reciprocating pumps are too slow. The pump is primed when in motion. Before starting a stripper pump make sure all the suction side and delivery side valves are open. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The suction and discharge valves of a positive displacement pump must always be open before starting the pump and must remain open until the pump is stopped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBXiv6DxPI/AAAAAAAACKI/1MTmrjcb_f0/s1600/RP2.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBXiv6DxPI/AAAAAAAACKI/1MTmrjcb_f0/s1600/RP2.JPG\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">These pumps must not be operated in excess of their designed speed and particular care must be taken to avoid these pumps over speeding when they lose suction.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">SCREW PUMPS</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"> \u2014they are self priming. The rotating elements are axially balanced and there is no metal to metal contact within the pump between the screws or the body . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBX4Xj2p3I/AAAAAAAACKM/e0gh6K5oEsQ/s1600/SP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBX4Xj2p3I/AAAAAAAACKM/e0gh6K5oEsQ/s1600/SP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">They can handle virtually any non homogeneous liquid regardless of viscosity and abrasiveness\u2014molasses, caustic soda, sea water , bitumen, clay slurry etc. generally used on a chemical tanker as a booster pump for molasses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/pojlbrrKEFo/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/pojlbrrKEFo&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/pojlbrrKEFo&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Screw pumps are rotary, positive displacement pumps that can have one or more screws to transfer high or low viscosity fluids along an axis typically screw pumps have two or more inter meshing screws rotating axially clockwise or counterclockwise. Each screw thread is matched to carry a specific volume of fluid The capacity of screw pumps can be calculated based on the dimensions of the pump, the dimensions of the surface of the screws, and the rotational speed of the rotor since a specific volume is transferred with each revolution.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBX-yf-8fI/AAAAAAAACKU/FovuZukNt00/s1600/SP3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBX-yf-8fI/AAAAAAAACKU/FovuZukNt00/s1600/SP3.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Screw pumps and piston pumps must have a bypass line and safety valve to protect the delivery line which may burst if the shore tank valve is not open. Positive displacement pumps like piston/ screw/ gear pumps are never started with delivery valve shut. The viscosity of the fluid transferred and the lift required may affect the speed and power required. Indicators of pump malfunction include decrease in flow rate or increased noise. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBYa3AdtpI/AAAAAAAACKY/o-2w_zBNhmI/s1600/SP4.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBYa3AdtpI/AAAAAAAACKY/o-2w_zBNhmI/s1600/SP4.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The efficiency of screw pumps requires that each rotor turns at a rate that allows each cavity to fill completely in order to work at full capacity--.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Low pulsation for smooth, quiet operation. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Direct-drive for design and operational simplicity.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Low shear for protection of the pumped fluid. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Hydraulic balance for minimal deflection and wear.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Cartridge-type rotating assembly for easy servicing.&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Integral relief valve to eliminate external valves and piping<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Built-in heat jacket to facilitate cold start. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Customized ports to adapt to the best piping arrangements for the system. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Selection of materials for the longest service life. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBX8ET1ytI/AAAAAAAACKQ/TQXolHv3Y-I/s1600/SP2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBX8ET1ytI/AAAAAAAACKQ/TQXolHv3Y-I/s1600/SP2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">It can handle a highly viscous liquid of up to 1,000,000 mPaS like treacle molasses of high Brix value , as well as a material that is almost non-fluidal. The liquid can be transferred smoothly without pulsation, stirring, or foaming.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/LEMfyUvQ-qw/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/LEMfyUvQ-qw&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/LEMfyUvQ-qw&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Furthermore, the flow rate can be controlled easily by adjusting the pump speed. The self-priming capability is maximum 9 m, making the pump ideal for assisting the deep well pump by sucking from underneath \u2013from the cargo tanks Drive is usually Framo powered \u2013they are able to withstand high temp and back pressures <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">EDUCTORS</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\"> </span>cannot strip cargo to shore due to its limited capacity to work against back pressure\u2014the drive flow has to be maintained. So you have to do internal stripping.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBY9vOc6PI/AAAAAAAACKc/RejLThbKgPU/s1600/ED3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBY9vOc6PI/AAAAAAAACKc/RejLThbKgPU/s1600/ED3.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Eductors must be operated at the full designed pressure\u2014or its efficiency becomes less. Open the eductor suction valve last and shut it first \u2014to prevent back flow, and also suction lines may not be strong enough to hold the pressure.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZC1G1N3I/AAAAAAAACKg/gsVa5zRL5rk/s1600/ED2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZC1G1N3I/AAAAAAAACKg/gsVa5zRL5rk/s1600/ED2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">When stopping an eductor the eductor suction valve should be closed before reducing the driving pressure and the tank suction valve should remain open until the eductor is stopped in order to avoid shutting down the piping system with a 'locked in' vacuum.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">If, during use, the eductor driving pressure falls below the operating pressure range, the eductor suction valve should be closed to prevent backflow of the driving liquid. The tank suction valve must not be used to prevent back flow as these valves and the suction piping may not be designed to withstand such high pressure.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object width=\"320\" height=\"266\" class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://2.gvt0.com/vi/8MvHplOIQCI/0.jpg\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/8MvHplOIQCI&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/8MvHplOIQCI&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Also portable eductors must be installed as low as possible.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"UsualBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-left: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt; text-indent: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">Operation of the eductor against a higher discharge head than the design discharge head&nbsp; has the effect of reducing the eductor's suction capacity.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZRT5FduI/AAAAAAAACKk/TcKcq0d9HCw/s1600/ED.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"116\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZRT5FduI/AAAAAAAACKk/TcKcq0d9HCw/s320/ED.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The eductor uses an internal nozzle to produce a vacuum within it. A driving liquid leaves the nozzle at high velocity producing a vacuum which draws in the liquid to be pumped, and expels it by transferring its kinetic energy. It can pump liquids vapour and impurities , as long as the nozzle does not get restricted. However a disadvantage is that the driving liquid must be compatible with the liquid to be pumped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoBodyText\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-bottom: 0in; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<b><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">VARIABLE DISPLACEMENT PUMPS</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"> The displacement can be adjusted to increase or decrease the amount of fluid pumped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZ4P3jxII/AAAAAAAACKo/1VvT0LXZadw/s1600/VD2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZ4P3jxII/AAAAAAAACKo/1VvT0LXZadw/s1600/VD2.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/2mh902AP7Yw/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/2mh902AP7Yw&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/2mh902AP7Yw&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">A common variable displacement pump is the axial piston pump. This pump has several pistons ( usually odd number ) in cylinders arranged parallel to each other and rotating around a central shaft. A swash plate at one end is connected to the pistons. As the pistons rotate, the angle of the plate causes them to move in and out of their cylinders. A rotary valve at the opposite end from the swash plate alternately connects each cylinder to the fluid supply and delivery lines.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBalH48vgI/AAAAAAAACK0/fFuwATI44rA/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBalH48vgI/AAAAAAAACK0/fFuwATI44rA/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">By changing the angle of the swash plate, the stroke of the pistons can be varied continuously. If the swash plate is perpendicular to the axis of rotation, no fluid will flow. If it is at a sharp angle, a large volume of fluid will be pumped. Some pumps allow the swash plate to be moved in both directions from the zero position, pumping fluid in either direction without reversing the rotation of the pump. By adjusting the position of the swash plate, variable displacement axial piston pump can vary flow smoothly, as flow is proportional to displacement. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZ-bWQ3kI/AAAAAAAACKs/ffzPwsHYVKQ/s1600/VD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBZ-bWQ3kI/AAAAAAAACKs/ffzPwsHYVKQ/s1600/VD.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">At maximum angle, displacement is at its highest because the pistons travel at maximum length. When the angle is reduced, piston travel shortens, reducing displacement. If flow remains constant, a motor runs faster, but torque is decreased. Torque is greatest at maximum displacement because the component of piston force parallel to a swash plate is greatest .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBaUAg_9pI/AAAAAAAACKw/xbJTcNv1OFg/s1600/VD3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TRBaUAg_9pI/AAAAAAAACKw/xbJTcNv1OFg/s1600/VD3.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">The FRAMO deepwell pump power pack pumps are of axial piston type , <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">swash plate </span>design with variable displacement. The pump displacement ( swivel angle ) is hydraulically controlled via the pressure regulator of each main pump.&nbsp; If the oil consumption is increased the swash plate is pushed to increased swivel angle until a new balance is reached between oil delivery and consumption. By this method oil delivery from the hydraulic pump will always be the same as oil consumption from hyd motors. In variable displacement pumps , by changing the angle of pump axis ( swivel angle ) delivery change can be effected. (angle between cyl block and shaft is varied ). Swivel angle of the pump is hydraulically controlled with spring centring via the control cylinder. A bigger angle will give more oil flow, but it will also require a bigger torque on the drive shaft to maintain the same pressure.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 115%;\">SLIDING VANE PUMP</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; tab-stops: 405.0pt;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/oMQ_HXUvg38/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/oMQ_HXUvg38&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/oMQ_HXUvg38&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\nROTARY LOBE PUMP<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Guidance of the relevant clause in the CP may be taken.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">Sometimes NOR is accepted only after the appointed surveyors have passes the tanks to be loaded. Hence Master must take initiative in getting tanks ready and asking these people to board ship as soon as feasible. NOR is issued even if the ship has to dischg SBT before commencing to load.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">If there is only one load/ dishcg berth with only one shipper consignee involved, only one NOR is required. If there are different shippers/ consignees at different berths , then a new NOR must be tendered for each berth, at the time of completion disconnecting hoses at the previous berth.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;If the Master is advised in advance that the berth is not available, he should proceed to arrival position at best speed as per CP and tender NOR at the earliest time. If the ship is told to adjust speed to save fuel , ensure this communication is preserved and projected in the time sheet, to avoid under performance speed claims after a couple of months<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%; margin-top: 8.0pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Tender NOR by email/ telex to charterers agent as soon as you arrive pilot station/ customary anchorage ( EOSP/ SBE ). NOR can be tendered at any hour by telex , fax or email. If there will be an anchorage is is better to tender NOR at anchor down time.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">Later on berthing tender NOR in the proper format as it is an important document for demurrage collection. NOR copy is of great use to charterers and the document should be sent to them. The written NOR is only a written record of the actual NOR tendered by e-mail / fax / telex to the appropriate authorities.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If there are 2 berths, as soon as the last hose is disconnected at the first berth, the agent will re-tender NOR to cargo interests at the second berth. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Arial&quot;,&quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: Batang;\">If cargo to be loaded is limited by dead weight or volume then MAXIMUM cargo loadable to be included.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" free pratique has been granted or tanks have been passed for loading.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" An ordinary man on the street can write good poetry. Good poetry means 90% of the people both erudite and illiterate who read it will be impressed.&nbsp;</span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\">The remaining 10% misanthropes of this planet , who need something other than poetry to get impressed, please excuse.<span style=\"font-size: x-small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; An ordinary man on the street can write good poetry.&nbsp;</span></span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-size: x-small;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">after six months of camping, in lonely avenue</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">wound up taut, &nbsp;like a high tension spring</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">suffering from the blues , when lonely winds blew past</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; , sans-serif;\">falling apart from the seams, &nbsp;when bad news came from home</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">yet, &nbsp;never allowing a sight to get out of his heart</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; , sans-serif;\">controlling his biological urges, &nbsp;being the perfect family man</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">changing coats constantly, &nbsp;as the situation on board deemed</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;
