, sans-serif;\">judge, doctor, policeman, accountant, pest control, cook</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">journalist , plumber, head shrink, soldier ( without license to kill )</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">businessman --you name it--he does it as part of his job</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">round the clock, not 9 to 5 -- day after day, without holiday</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">giving away prizes, which he , and only he had earned</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">yet, willingly being the scapegoat , when murphy's law ruled</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">trying to figure out the blurred line between fact and fiction</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">living on the edge, never feelin' immune to the prospect of failure</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">working for bosses who had mastered the art of exploiting vulnerability</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">steeling himself to read telexes which started -- \"we fail to understand--\"</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">being the punching bag for thankless owners , managers and charterers</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">being forced to take uncalculated risks, against his better judgement</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">trying to push his ship, to keep pace with a pea brained schedule</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">pushing mr.pride aside, &nbsp;when dealing with customs and coastguard</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">itching to bloody their noses , but somehow, &nbsp;holding his peace</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">forcing him to add more names, to the list of people who could kiss his ass</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">being patient to wait for one more minute, past eternity</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">dealing with faceless men, and spineless backdoor hustlers</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">who got their kicks ,by sending missiles by telex from overseas</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">rubbing shoulders with powers that be , who put their mouths into motion</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">without putting their collective brains into gear --even once</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">deadening his raw nerves in the cold comfort of whisky heaven</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">--the days his bosses played petty mind games of domination on him</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">distrusting angels which fly too low-- not believing in messiahs</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; , sans-serif;\">burning bridges behind him , when the situation became 'no go'</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">combating the sinkin' feeling that time is running out on him</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">time and again, counting the odds against tomorrow</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">wearing lucky charms , combating ulcers and nose bleeds</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">yet thriving on the virus of pressure , like the quintessential shark</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">which need to suck salt water past its gills to stay alive</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">after all this--</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">this modern seafarin' gypsy has passed on his crown of thorns</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">packed his bags, &nbsp;and is now a stranger in even stranger lands</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">destination home-sweet-home, his DTGH is only one</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">wending his weary way to his hotel room, he drops on the bed</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">the windmills of his mind come to a smooth halt , as he falls into slumber</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">they had been ceaselessly turned by winds of anxiety, the last six months</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">it is unwinding time now for this poor wanderer</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">HUSH!&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">NOT A SOUND!! &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">THE CAPTAIN SLEEPS TONIGHT!!!</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8E3Ecj0rI/AAAAAAAACGY/2vPhiInjel0/s1600/UID.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8E3Ecj0rI/AAAAAAAACGY/2vPhiInjel0/s1600/UID.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Such a catchy slogan of an ideal India where different communities, races, religions, languages and cultural groups co-exist in harmony .</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Communalism in India is the major cause of violence and intolerance in modern times (however we do tend to unite in times of external threat) .</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ94Ye7Dk4I/AAAAAAAACIA/Si1f0s4T8ig/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ94Ye7Dk4I/AAAAAAAACIA/Si1f0s4T8ig/s1600/images+%25289%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;Intolerance was the reason why British was able to \"divide and rule\" India for centuries.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8ETD-RDvI/AAAAAAAACGU/BPR88SFRkHc/s1600/NX.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8ETD-RDvI/AAAAAAAACGU/BPR88SFRkHc/s1600/NX.JPG\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Our enemies and anti national elements are able to create separatist tendencies and communal feelings easily. Lawlessness and Naxalism are on the rise. We have not shown the will to crush these disruptive separatist forces with an iron hand, due to vote bank politics and ruthless politicians being voted into the Parliament.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8Jsc0WlqI/AAAAAAAACHI/15oNcsraAYk/s1600/POL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8Jsc0WlqI/AAAAAAAACHI/15oNcsraAYk/s1600/POL.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">There are foreign powers fanning flames of communalism, racialism, provincialism , lingualism and casteism because they are jealous of our fast rise as a financial and military power. They fund Judas NGOs in India to be their instruments of subversion. They have their stooges coming on TV news channels&nbsp;funded by them on prime time to sow seeds of suspicion between castes and sects of Indian people.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">For national integration it is important that we the people give up communal and sectarian outlooks. We should be Indians first and Indians last.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ94HUM9AAI/AAAAAAAACH8/c0lzd4X8o4s/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ94HUM9AAI/AAAAAAAACH8/c0lzd4X8o4s/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">It is important to remove the divide between haves and have-nots and reduce unemployment, to give hope to the down trodden . Justice must be swift and fair.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8JdRObN7I/AAAAAAAACHE/97DfqXtk1kc/s1600/UNE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8JdRObN7I/AAAAAAAACHE/97DfqXtk1kc/s1600/UNE.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Narrow minded language groups behave in a chauvinistic manner and have launched hate movements on the basis of son of the soil theory. An example is the \u201cMarati Manoos\u201c agitation in Maharshtra with the champions of hatred and their perpetrators behaving as if they are a law by themselves.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8Mik92W2I/AAAAAAAACHM/oSaqwG2DF7o/s1600/MNS.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8Mik92W2I/AAAAAAAACHM/oSaqwG2DF7o/s1600/MNS.JPG\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The Cauvery water dispute riots saw many fall victim to meaningless riots.&nbsp;A lot of regional parties have cropped up in India who tilt the power balance , when a government has to be formed with full 2/3 majority.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;In the last elections a big chunk of the candidates were known criminals.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ93oe-B6MI/AAAAAAAACH4/0Q0Uhhc8nko/s1600/download+%25282%2529.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ93oe-B6MI/AAAAAAAACH4/0Q0Uhhc8nko/s1600/download+%25282%2529.JPG\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Election manifestos are made to win the election with cheap gimmicks like free colour TV\u2019s\u2014with the needs of the country and society totally ignored.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">There is another mini India in the north east part where the people have never been considered in the mainstream and have been alienated -- just because they don\u2019t look like the rest of us .&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8NV8XQOlI/AAAAAAAACHQ/1sUb6UR53hE/s1600/BB.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8NV8XQOlI/AAAAAAAACHQ/1sUb6UR53hE/s1600/BB.JPG\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Most of these areas do not have basic facilities. Seething with discontent they have taken to militancy.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">The Naxalism movement has risen due to neglect of backward people in mineral and forest rich regions. Politics of regionalism has degenerated into militancy and&nbsp;terrorism, with our external enemies providing them with weapons and training.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ93WSKH5yI/AAAAAAAACH0/N-6zkoBS2DU/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ93WSKH5yI/AAAAAAAACH0/N-6zkoBS2DU/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Religion must never be allowed to mix with politics. Rulers now use religion to hold absolute power. It has become a drug -- more potent can any intoxicant.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8I4x0tCdI/AAAAAAAACHA/x5FR5EQG5wQ/s1600/POW.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8I4x0tCdI/AAAAAAAACHA/x5FR5EQG5wQ/s1600/POW.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">Caste system must be eradicated , whose roots lie in the law of inequality. Every society in India is caste ridden . Even Christians and Muslims cannot go to just any church or mosque they feel like.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">T</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">here are about 140 castes in Kerala Christianity and 10 castes among Muslims. Latin catholic, Syrian catholic , Pentecost, Salvation army, Marthoma, 7<sup>th</sup>&nbsp;day Adventist, Orthodox, Jacobite churches do not want others to wander in and pray. Every caste has its own rituals and self imposed restrictions.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8FaJQ5lEI/AAAAAAAACGc/6eZfMoA0hKI/s1600/APP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8FaJQ5lEI/AAAAAAAACGc/6eZfMoA0hKI/s1600/APP.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">We now have reservation policies, where the divide is made wider, with merit taking a severe beating. The caste system must die, for India to progress and know peace.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8INnVLTqI/AAAAAAAACG8/V87uegxguRs/s1600/CASTE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8INnVLTqI/AAAAAAAACG8/V87uegxguRs/s1600/CASTE.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">We in Kerala like to boast of our high literacy and high tech health facilities. Most of this feel good factor is because of the regular NRI money inflow. Take this aside and what you see is dirty politics and trade unionism.&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8IBXzmNKI/AAAAAAAACG4/qNj31tAevuI/s1600/HAR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQ8IBXzmNKI/AAAAAAAACG4/qNj31tAevuI/s1600/HAR.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;\">There is hardly any leader of stature whom people can respect. </span>follo<span style=\"letter-spacing: 0.05pt;\">w</span>ing<span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.4pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -0.1pt;\">t</span><span style=\"letter-spacing:
